<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">3.8</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Ref512395916"></a><a name="_Toc530231078"></a><a name="_Toc472884918"></a><a name="_Toc127111419"></a><a name="_Toc130134161"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">QUORUM; VOTING</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">At all meetings of the board of directors, a majority of the total authorized number of directors shall constitute a quorum for the transaction of business. If a quorum is not present at any meeting of the board of directors, then the directors present thereat may adjourn the meeting from time to time, without notice other than announcement at the meeting, until a quorum is present. A meeting at which a quorum is initially present may continue to transact business notwithstanding the withdrawal of directors, if any action taken is approved by at least a majority of the required quorum for that meeting.</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">19</a></p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="sty_hc_18"></a><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The vote of a majority of the directors </font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">present</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"> at any meeting at which a quorum is present shall be the act of the board of directors, except as may be otherwise specifically provided by statute, the certificate of incorporation or these bylaws. In the event a director or directors abstain or are disqualified from a vote, the majority vote of the director or the directors thereof not abstaining or disqualified from voting, </font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">whether or not</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="sty_hc_18"></a> such director or directors constitute a quorum, shall be the act of the board of directors.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU16"></a>If the certificate of incorporation provides that one or more directors shall have more or less than one vote per director on any matter, every reference in these bylaws to a majority or other proportion of the directors shall refer to a majority or other proportion of the votes of the directors.</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">3.9</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Ref512395982"></a><a name="_Toc530231079"></a><a name="_Toc472884919"></a><a name="_Toc127111420"></a><a name="_Toc130134162"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">BOARD ACTION BY WRITTEN CONSENT WITHOUT A MEETING</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Unless otherwise restricted by the certificate of incorporation or these bylaws, any action required or permitted to be taken at any meeting of the board of directors, or of any committee thereof, may be taken without a meeting if all members of the board of directors or committee, as the case may be, consent thereto in writing or by electronic transmission and the writing or writings or electronic transmission or transmissions are filed with the minutes of proceedings of the board of directors or committee. Such filing shall be in paper form if the minutes are maintained in paper form and shall be in electronic form if the minutes are maintained in electronic form.</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">3.10</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc530231080"></a><a name="_Toc472884920"></a><a name="_Toc127111421"></a><a name="_Toc130134163"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">FEES AND COMPENSATION OF DIRECTORS</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Unless otherwise restricted by the certificate of incorporation or these bylaws, the board of directors shall have the authority to fix the compensation of directors.</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">3.11</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc530231082"></a><a name="_Toc472884921"></a><a name="_Toc127111422"></a><a name="_Toc130134164"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">REMOVAL OF DIRECTORS</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">A director may be removed from office by the stockholders of the corporation only for cause.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">No reduction of the authorized number of directors shall have the effect of removing any director prior to the expiration of such director&#8217;s term of office.</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:uppercase;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><a name="_Toc530231083"></a><a name="_Toc472884922"></a><a name="_Toc127111423"></a><a name="_Toc130134165"></a><a name="sty_ht1_11"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;">Article&#160;IV&#160;&#8212;</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;color:#000000;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">COMMITTEES</font></p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">4.1</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc530231084"></a><a name="_Toc472884923"></a><a name="_Toc127111424"></a><a name="_Toc130134166"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">COMMITTEES OF DIRECTORS</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="sty_hc_19"></a>The board of directors may designate one or more committees, each committee to consist of one or more of the directors of the corporation. The board of directors may designate one or more directors as alternate members of any committee, who may replace any absent or disqualified member at any meeting of the committee. In the absence or disqualification of a member of a committee, the member or members thereof present at any meeting and not disqualified from voting, whether or not such member or members constitute a quorum, may unanimously appoint another member of the board of directors to act at the meeting in the place of any such absent or disqualified member. In the event a member or members of a committee abstain or are disqualified from a vote, the majority vote of the member or members thereof not abstaining or disqualified from voting, whether or not such member or members constitute a quorum, shall be the act of such </p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">20</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">committee. Any such committee, to the extent provided in the resolution of the board of directors or in these bylaws, shall have and may exercise all the powers and authority of the board of directors in the management of the business and affairs of the corporation, and may authorize the seal of the corporation to be affixed to all papers that may require it; but no such committee shall have the power or authority to (</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">i</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="sty_hc_19"></a>) approve or adopt, or recommend to the stockholders, any action or matter (other than the election or removal of directors) expressly required by the DGCL to be submitted to stockholders for approval, or (ii) adopt, amend or repeal any bylaw of the corporation.</font></p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">4.2</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc530231085"></a><a name="_Toc472884924"></a><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU17"></a><a name="_Toc127111425"></a><a name="_Toc130134167"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">COMMITTEE MINUTES</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Each committee shall keep regular minutes of its meetings and report the same to the board of directors when required.</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">4.3</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc530231086"></a><a name="_Toc472884925"></a><a name="_Toc127111426"></a><a name="_Toc130134168"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">MEETINGS AND ACTION OF COMMITTEES</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Meetings and actions of committees shall be governed by, and held and taken in accordance with, the provisions of:</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:15.38%;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;">(i)</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;color:#000000;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">Section 3.5 (place of meetings and meetings by telephone);</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:15.38%;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;">(ii)</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;color:#000000;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">Section 3.6 (regular meetings);</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:15.38%;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;">(iii)</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;color:#000000;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">Section 3.7 (special meetings; notice);</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:15.38%;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;">(iv)</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;color:#000000;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">Section 3.8 (quorum; voting); </font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:15.38%;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;">(v)</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;color:#000000;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">Section 3.9 (action without a meeting); and</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:15.38%;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;">(vi)</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;color:#000000;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">Section 7.5 (waiver of notice)</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">with such changes in the context of those bylaws as are necessary to substitute the committee and its members for the board of directors and its members. <font style="font-style:italic;">However</font>:</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:15.38%;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;">(i)</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;color:#000000;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">the time of regular meetings of committees may be determined by resolution of the committee; </font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:15.38%;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;">(ii)</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;color:#000000;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">special meetings of committees may also be called by resolution of the committee; and </font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:15.38%;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;">(iii)</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;color:#000000;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">notice of special meetings of committees shall also be given to all alternate members, who shall have the right to attend all meetings of the committee. The board of directors may adopt rules for the government of any committee not inconsistent with the provisions of these bylaws.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Any provision in the certificate of incorporation providing that one or more directors shall have more or less than one vote per director on any matter shall apply to voting in any committee or subcommittee, unless otherwise provided in the certificate of incorporation or these bylaws.</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">21</a></p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">4.4</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc472884926"></a><a name="_Toc127111427"></a><a name="_Toc130134169"></a><font style="text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;"></font><font style="color:#000000;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">SUBCOMMITTEES</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="sty_hc_20"></a>Unless otherwise provided in the certificate of incorporation, these bylaws<a name="sty_hc_20"></a> or the resolutions of the board of directors designating the committee, a committee may create one or more subcommittees, each subcommittee to consist of one or more members of the committee, and delegate to a subcommittee any or all of the powers and authority of the committee.</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:uppercase;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><a name="_Toc530231087"></a><a name="_Toc472884927"></a><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU18"></a><a name="_Toc127111428"></a><a name="_Toc130134170"></a><a name="sty_ht1_12"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;">Article&#160;V&#160;&#8212;</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;color:#000000;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">OFFICERS</font></p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">5.1</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc530231088"></a><a name="_Toc472884928"></a><a name="_Toc127111429"></a><a name="_Toc130134171"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">OFFICERS</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The officers of the corporation shall be a president and a secretary. The corporation may also have, at the discretion of the board of directors, a chairperson of the board of directors, a vice chairperson of the board of directors, a chief executive officer, a chief financial officer or treasurer, one or more vice presidents, one or more assistant vice presidents, one or more assistant treasurers, one or more assistant secretaries, and any such other officers as may be appointed in accordance with the provisions of these bylaws. Any number of offices may be held by the same person. </p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">5.2</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Ref519419198"></a><a name="_Toc530231089"></a><a name="_Toc472884929"></a><a name="_Toc127111430"></a><a name="_Toc130134172"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">APPOINTMENT OF OFFICERS</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The board of directors shall appoint the officers of the corporation, except such officers as may be appointed in accordance with the provisions of Section 5.3 of these bylaws, subject to the rights, if any, of an officer under any contract of employment. A vacancy in any office because of death, resignation, removal, disqualification or any other cause shall be filled in the manner prescribed in this Section 5 for the regular election to such office.</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">5.3</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc127111431"></a><a name="_Toc130134173"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">SUBORDINATE OFFICERS</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The board of directors may appoint, or empower the chief executive officer or, in the absence of a chief executive officer, the president, to appoint, such other officers and agents as the business of the corporation may require. Each of such officers and agents shall hold office for such period, have such authority, and perform such duties as are provided in these bylaws or as the board of directors may from time to time determine.</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">5.4</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc530231091"></a><a name="_Toc472884931"></a><a name="_Toc127111432"></a><a name="_Toc130134174"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">REMOVAL AND RESIGNATION OF OFFICERS</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Subject to the rights, if any, of an officer under any contract of employment, any officer may be removed, either with or without cause, by an affirmative vote of the majority of the board of directors at any regular or special meeting of the board of directors or, except in the case of an officer chosen by the board of directors, by any officer upon whom such power of removal may be conferred by the board of directors.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Any officer may resign at any time by giving written or electronic notice to the corporation; <font style="font-style:italic;">provided, however</font>, that if such notice is given by electronic transmission, such electronic transmission must either set forth or be submitted with information from which it can be determined that the electronic transmission was authorized by the officer. Any resignation shall take effect at the date of the receipt of that notice or at any later time specified in that notice. Unless otherwise specified in the notice of resignation, the acceptance of the resignation shall not be </p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">22</a></p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">necessary to make it effective. Any resignation is without prejudice to the rights, if any, of the corporation under any contract to which the officer is a party.</font></p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">5.5</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Ref519419165"></a><a name="_Toc530231092"></a><a name="_Toc472884932"></a><a name="_Toc127111433"></a><a name="_Toc130134175"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">VACANCIES IN OFFICES</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="sty_hc_21"></a><a name="sty_hc_21"></a>Any vacancy occurring in any office of the corporation shall be filled by the board of directors or as provided in Section 5.3.</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">5.6</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc530231093"></a><a name="_Toc472884933"></a><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU19"></a><a name="_Toc127111434"></a><a name="_Toc130134176"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">REPRESENTATION OF SHARES OF OTHER CORPORATIONS</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The chairperson of the board of directors, the president, any vice president, the treasurer, the secretary or assistant secretary of this corporation, or any other person authorized by the board of directors or the president or a vice president, is authorized to vote, represent, and exercise on behalf of this corporation all rights incident to any and all shares of any other corporation or corporations standing in the name of this corporation. The authority granted herein may be exercised either by such person directly or by any other person authorized to do so by proxy or power of attorney duly executed by such person having the authority.</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">5.7</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc530231094"></a><a name="_Toc472884934"></a><a name="_Toc127111435"></a><a name="_Toc130134177"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">AUTHORITY AND DUTIES OF OFFICERS</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">All officers of the corporation shall respectively have such authority and perform such duties in the management of the business of the corporation as may be designated from time to time by the board of directors and, to the extent not so provided, as generally pertain to their respective offices, subject to the control of the board of directors.</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">5.8</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc472884935"></a><a name="_Toc127111436"></a><a name="_Toc130134178"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">THE CHAIRPERSON OF THE BOARD</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The chairperson of the board shall have the powers and duties customarily and usually associated with the office of the chairperson of the board. The chairperson of the board shall preside at meetings of the stockholders and of the board of directors.</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">5.9</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc472884936"></a><a name="_Toc127111437"></a><a name="_Toc130134179"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">THE VICE CHAIRPERSON OF THE BOARD</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The vice chairperson of the board shall have the powers and duties customarily and usually associated with the office of the vice chairperson of the board. In the case of absence or disability of the chairperson of the board, the vice chairperson of the board shall perform the duties and exercise the powers of the chairperson of the board.</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">5.10</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc472884937"></a><a name="_Toc127111438"></a><a name="_Toc130134180"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">THE CHIEF EXECUTIVE OFFICER</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The chief executive officer shall have, subject to the supervision, direction and control of the board of directors, ultimate authority for decisions relating to the supervision, direction and management of the affairs and the business of the corporation customarily and usually associated with the position of chief executive officer, including, without limitation, all powers necessary to direct and control the organizational and reporting relationships within the corporation. If at any time the office of the chairperson and vice chairperson of the board shall not be filled, or in the event of the temporary absence or disability of the chairperson of the board and the vice </p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">23</a></p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">chairperson of the board, the chief executive officer shall perform the duties and exercise the powers of the chairperson of the board unless otherwise determined by the board of directors.</font></p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">5.11</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc472884938"></a><a name="_Toc127111439"></a><a name="_Toc130134181"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">THE PRESIDENT</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU20"></a>The president shall have, subject to the supervision, direction and control of the board of directors, the general powers and duties of supervision, direction and management of the affairs and business of the corporation customarily and usually associated with the position of president. The president shall have such powers and perform such duties as may from time to time be assigned to him or her by the board of directors, the chairperson of the board or the chief executive officer. In the event of the absence or disability of the chief executive officer, the president shall perform the duties and exercise the powers of the chief executive officer unless otherwise determined by the board of directors.</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">5.12</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc472884939"></a><a name="_Toc127111440"></a><a name="_Toc130134182"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">THE VICE PRESIDENTS AND ASSISTANT VICE PRESIDENTS</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Each vice president and assistant vice president shall have such powers and perform such duties as may from time to time be assigned to him or her by the board of directors, the chairperson of the board, the chief executive officer or the president.</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">5.13</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc472884940"></a><a name="_Toc127111441"></a><a name="_Toc130134183"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">THE SECRETARY AND ASSISTANT SECRETARIES</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:15.38%;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;">(i)</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;color:#000000;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">The secretary shall attend meetings of the board of directors and meetings of the stockholders and record all votes and minutes of all such proceedings in a book or books kept for such purpose. The secretary shall have all such further powers and duties as are customarily and usually associated with the position of secretary or as may from time to time be assigned to him or her by the board of directors, the chairperson of the board, the chief executive officer or the president.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:15.38%;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;">(ii)</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;color:#000000;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">Each assistant secretary shall have such powers and perform such duties as may from time to time be assigned to him or her by the board of directors, the chairperson of the board, the chief executive officer, the president or the secretary. In the event of the absence, inability or refusal to act of the secretary, the assistant secretary (or if there shall be more than one, the assistant secretaries in the order determined by the board of directors) shall perform the duties and exercise the powers of the secretary.</font></p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">5.14</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc472884941"></a><a name="_Toc127111442"></a><a name="_Toc130134184"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">THE CHIEF FINANCIAL OFFICER AND ASSISTANT TREASURERS</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:15.38%;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;">(i)</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;color:#000000;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">The chief financial officer shall be the treasurer of the corporation. The chief financial officer shall have custody of the corporation&#8217;s funds and securities, shall be responsible for maintaining the corporation&#8217;s accounting records and statements, shall keep full and accurate accounts of receipts and disbursements in books belonging to the corporation, and shall deposit or cause to be deposited moneys or other valuable effects in the name and to the credit of the corporation in such depositories as may be designated by the board of directors. The chief financial officer shall also maintain adequate records of all assets, liabilities and transactions of the corporation and shall assure that adequate audits thereof are currently and regularly made. The chief financial officer shall have all such further powers and duties as are customarily and usually </font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">24</a></p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="color:#000000;">associated with the position of chief financial officer, or as may from time to time be assigned to him or her by the board of directors, the chairperson, the chief executive </font><font style="color:#000000;">officer</font><font style="color:#000000;"> or the president.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:15.38%;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><a name="sty_hc_23"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;">(ii)</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;color:#000000;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">Each assistant treasurer shall have such powers and perform such duties as may from time to time be assigned to him or her by the board of directors, the chief executive officer, the president or the chief financial officer. In the event of the absence, inability<a name="sty_hc_23"></a> or refusal to act of the chief financial officer, the assistant treasurer (or if there shall be more than one, the assistant treasurers in the order determined by the board of directors) shall perform the duties and exercise the powers of the chief financial officer.</font></p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:0%;font-weight:bold;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:uppercase;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><a name="_Toc472884942"></a><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU21"></a><a name="_Toc127111443"></a><a name="_Toc130134185"></a><a name="sty_ht1_13"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;">Article&#160;VI&#160;&#8212;</font><font style="margin-left:36pt;color:#000000;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">STOCK</font></p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">6.1</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc530231100"></a><a name="_Toc472884943"></a><a name="_Toc127111444"></a><a name="_Toc130134186"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">STOCK CERTIFICATES; PARTLY PAID SHARES</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The shares of the corporation shall be represented by certificates, provided that the board of directors may provide by resolution or resolutions that some or all of any or all classes or series of its stock shall be uncertificated shares. Any such resolution shall not apply to shares represented by a certificate until such certificate is surrendered to the corporation. Every holder of stock represented by certificates shall be entitled to have a certificate signed by, or in the name of the corporation by the chairperson of the board of directors or vice-chairperson of the board of directors, or the president or a vice-president, and by the treasurer or an assistant treasurer, or the secretary or an assistant secretary of the corporation representing the number of shares registered in certificate form. Any or all of the signatures on the certificate may be a facsimile. In case any officer, transfer agent or registrar who has signed or whose facsimile signature has been placed upon a certificate has ceased to be such officer, transfer agent or registrar before such certificate is issued, it may be issued by the corporation with the same effect as if such person were such officer, transfer agent or registrar at the date of issue. The corporation shall not have power to issue a certificate in bearer form.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The corporation may issue the whole or any part of its shares as partly paid and subject to call for the remainder of the consideration to be paid therefor. Upon the face or back of each stock certificate issued to represent any such partly-paid shares, or upon the books and records of the corporation in the case of uncertificated partly-paid shares, the total amount of the consideration to be paid therefor and the amount paid thereon shall be stated. Upon the declaration of any dividend on fully-paid shares, the corporation shall declare a dividend upon partly-paid shares of the same class, but only upon the basis of the percentage of the consideration actually paid thereon.</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">6.2</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc530231101"></a><a name="_Ref177550847"></a><a name="_Toc472884944"></a><a name="_Toc127111445"></a><a name="_Toc130134187"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">SPECIAL DESIGNATION ON CERTIFICATES</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="sty_hc_24"></a>If the corporation is authorized to issue more than one class of stock or more than one series of any class, then the powers, the designations, the preferences, and the relative, participating, optional or other special rights of each class of stock or series thereof and the qualifications, limitations or restrictions of such preferences and/or rights shall be set forth in full or summarized on the face or back of the certificate that the corporation shall issue to represent such class or series of stock; <font style="font-style:italic;">provided, however</font>, that, except as otherwise provided in Section 202 of the DGCL, in lieu of the foregoing requirements there may be set forth on the face or back of the certificate that the corporation shall issue to represent such class or series of stock, a statement that the corporation </p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">25</p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">will furnish without charge to each stockholder who so requests the powers, designations, preferences and relative, participating, optional or other special rights of each class of stock or series thereof and the qualifications, limitations or restrictions of such preferences and/or rights. Within a reasonable time after the issuance or transfer of uncertificated stock, the corporation shall send to the registered owner thereof a written notice containing the information required to be set forth or stated on certificates pursuant to this section 6.2 or Sections 156, 202(a) or 218(a) of the DGCL or with respect to this section 6.2 a statement that the corporation will furnish without charge to each stockholder who so requests the powers, designations, preferences and relative, participating, optional or other special rights of each class of stock or series thereof and the qualifications, limitations or restrictions of such preferences and/or rights. Except as otherwise expressly provided by law, the </font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">rights</font><font style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;"><a name="sty_hc_24"></a> and obligations of the holders of uncertificated stock and the rights and obligations of the holders of certificates representing stock of the same class and series shall be identical.</font></p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">6.3</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc530231102"></a><a name="_Ref109105041"></a><a name="_Toc472884945"></a><a name="_AEIOULastRenderedPageBreakAEIOU22"></a><a name="_Toc127111446"></a><a name="_Toc130134188"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">LOST, STOLEN OR DESTROYED CERTIFICATES</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Except as provided in this Section 6.3, no new certificates for shares shall be issued to replace a previously issued certificate unless the latter is surrendered to the corporation and cancelled at the same time. The corporation may issue a new certificate of stock or uncertificated shares in the place of any certificate theretofore issued by it, alleged to have been lost, stolen or destroyed, and the corporation may require the owner of the lost, stolen or destroyed certificate, or such owner&#8217;s legal representative, to give the corporation a bond sufficient to indemnify it against any claim that may be made against it on account of the alleged loss, theft or destruction of any such certificate or the issuance of such new certificate or uncertificated shares.</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">6.4</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc127111447"></a><a name="_Toc130134189"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">DIVIDENDS</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The board of directors, subject to any restrictions contained in the certificate of incorporation or applicable law, may declare and pay dividends upon the shares of the corporation&#8217;s capital stock. Dividends may be paid in cash, in property, or in shares of the corporation&#8217;s capital stock, subject to the provisions of the certificate of incorporation.</p>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">The board of directors may set apart out of any of the funds of the corporation available for dividends a reserve or reserves for any proper purpose and may abolish any such reserve. Such purposes shall include but not be limited to equalizing dividends, repairing or maintaining any property of the corporation, and meeting contingencies.</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p></td>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;"><font style="font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-decoration:none;Background-color:#auto;color:#000000;font-size:12pt;font-family:Times New Roman;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;">6.5</font></p></td>
<td valign="top">
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;color:#000000;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;letter-spacing:0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;"><a name="_Toc530231107"></a><a name="_Toc472884947"></a><a name="_Toc127111448"></a><a name="_Toc130134190"></a><font style="Background-color:#auto;text-decoration:none;"></font><font style="color:#000000;">TRANSFER OF STOCK</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
<p style="text-align:justify;margin-bottom:12pt;margin-top:12pt;text-indent:7.69%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">Transfers of record of shares of stock of the corporation shall be made only upon its books by the holders thereof, in person or by an attorney duly authorized, and, if such stock is certificated, upon the surrender of a certificate or certificates for a like number of shares, properly endorsed or accompanied by proper evidence of succession, assignation or authority to transfer; <font style="font-style:italic;">provided, however,</font> that such succession, assignment or authority to transfer is not prohibited by the certificate of incorporation, these bylaws, applicable law or contract.</p>
<p style="text-align:center;margin-top:12pt;margin-bottom:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;font-weight:normal;font-style:normal;text-transform:none;font-variant: normal;">26</a></p>
<hr style="page-break-after:always;width:100%;">
<p style="margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;text-indent:0%;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:12pt;">&nbsp;</p>
<div align="left">
<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0"  style="border-collapse:collapse; width:100%;">
<tr>
<td valign="top" style="width:7.69%;white-space:nowrap">
